It takes more than 1000 variants. root cause is that currently the search will continue
until the target is cleaned up from board if target block is dead.

Improvement idea: we search to the state where no way to make too eyes and only limited breath
without chance of extension, and enemy block is either live or having more breath.
That means once no way to make two eyes, we switch to breath race model.
